<script type="text/javascript">
GALFSRAM.jQuery(function() {
	var widget = GALFSRAM.jQuery("#MF_form_phrase").autocomplete({
		source: function(request, response) {
			GALFSRAM.jQuery.ajax({
				url: "suggest.x",
				dataType: "jsonp",
				data: {
					q: request.term,
					ie:"utf8",
					max:10
				},
				success: function( data ) {
					if (data.length > 0) {
						response(GALFSRAM.jQuery.each(data, function(index, e) {
							e.label = e.word;
							return e;
					}));
					}
				}
			});
		},
		appendTo: "#mf_searchbox",
		response: function (event, ui) {
		}
	}).data("ui-autocomplete");

	widget._renderItem = function( ul, item ) {
		var li = GALFSRAM.jQuery("<li>");
		li.append(GALFSRAM.jQuery("<a>").attr("href","search.x?q=" + encodeURI(item.word) ).text( item.word ));
		li.append(GALFSRAM.jQuery("<img src='/mf2file/custom/common.rs/0005/img/common/mf_addkeyword.png' width='16' height='16' onClick='clusterCheck(this);return false;' />"));
		return li.appendTo(ul);
	};

	widget._resizeMenu= function() {
                 var ul = this.menu.element;
                 ul.outerWidth( GALFSRAM.jQuery("#mf_searchbox").width() );
	};

});

function clusterCheck(target){
		GALFSRAM.jQuery("#MF_form_phrase").val("");
		GALFSRAM.jQuery("#MF_form_phrase").val(GALFSRAM.jQuery(target).prev().text() + " ");
		GALFSRAM.jQuery("#MF_form_phrase").trigger("keydown");
}

</script>

		});

			var mojiLength = GALFSRAM.jQuery("#MF_form_phrase").val().length;
			if(mojiLength > 0){
				GALFSRAM.jQuery("#clearText").css("display","block");
			}else{
				GALFSRAM.jQuery("#clearText").css("display","none");
			}
		 });
	});
</script>

(function($){

		var li = $(e).parent().parent().toggleClass("mf_close");
		var closed = String(li.attr('class')).match(/mf_close/);
		var img = $(e).children("img");

			img.attr('alt', "close");
			$(e).attr('title', "close");
		}
		return false;
	}  
})(GALFSRAM.jQuery);
